Goals</strong></h3><ul><li><strong>Objective</strong>: Predict whether a patient has a cardiovascular disease based on input features.</li><li><strong>Type of Problem</strong>: Classification (binary or multiclass).</li></ul><hr><h3>2. <strong>Prepare the Data</strong></h3><h4>a. <strong>Collect Data</strong></h4><ul><li>Obtain a relevant dataset (e.g., UCI Heart Disease dataset, Kaggle needed.</li></ul><h4>c. <strong>Feature Selection</strong></h4><ul><li>Identify important features such as age, cholesterol levels, blood pressure, etc.</li></ul><h4>d. <strong>Split the data = pd.read_csv(<span class="hljs-string">"cardiovascular_data.csv"</span>)

<span class="hljs-comment"># Separate features and target</span>
X = data.drop(<span class="hljs-string">"target"</span>, axis=<span class="hljs-number">1</span>)  <span class="hljs-comment"># Features</span>
y = data[<span class="hljs-string">"target"</span>]  <span class="hljs-comment"># Target variable</span>

<span class="hljs-comment"># Split the dataset</span>
X_train, X_test, y_train, y_test = train_test_split(X, y, test_size=<span class="hljs-number">0.2</span>, random_state=<span class="hljs-number">42</span>)

<span class="hljs-comment"># Normalize/Standardize features</span>
scaler = StandardScaler()
X_train = scaler.fit_transform(X_train)
X_test = scaler.transform(X_test)
</code></div></div></pre><h4>c. <strong>Train the Model</strong></h4><pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">python</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-python"><span class="hljs-comment"># Initialize and train the model</span>

Here's a detailed explanation:</p><hr><h3><strong>Breaking Down the Code</strong></h3><ol><li><p><strong><code>model_version = 1</code></strong></p><ul><li>This sets a version number for your model. You can increment this value to keep track of different versions of your model.</li></ul></li><li><p><strong><code>model.save()</code></strong></p><ul><li>This function is used to save a trained model to a file.</li><li>In TensorFlow/Keras, <code>model.save()</code> saves the model architecture, weights, and training configuration (optimizer, loss, metrics).</li></ul></li><li><p><strong><code>f"./models{model_version}"</code></strong></p><ul><li>This is an <strong>f-string</strong> in Python, which allows you to include variables directly in a string.</li><li>It creates a file path where the model will be saved. In this case, the path will be <code>./models1</code> for <code>model_version = 1</code>.</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>File Format</strong></p><ul><li>By default, <code>model.save()</code> saves the model in the TensorFlow SavedModel format.</li><li>If you append <code>.h5</code> to the filename (e.g., <code>f"./models{model_version}.h5"</code>), it saves the model in HDF5 format, which is a single-file format.</li></ul></li></ol><hr><h3><strong>Why Use Model Versioning?</strong></h3><ul><li><strong>Version Control</strong>: It helps you keep track of multiple versions of your model (e.g., <code>models1</code>, <code>models2</code>, etc.).</li><li><strong>Reproducibility</strong>: You can revisit previous versions of your model to compare performance or debug issues.</li><li><strong>Deployment</strong>: When deploying models, versioning is critical to ensure smooth updates without breaking the application.</li></ul><hr><h3><strong>Improved Example</strong></h3><pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> tensorflow.keras.layers <span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> Dense

<span class="hljs-comment"># Define and train a simple model</span>
model = Sequential([
    Dense(<span class="hljs-number">10</span>, input_shape=(<span class="hljs-number">20</span>,), activation=<span class="hljs-string">'relu'</span>),
    Dense(<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, activation=<span class="hljs-string">'sigmoid'</span>)
])
model.<span class="hljs-built_in">compile</span>(optimizer=<span class="hljs-string">'adam'</span>, loss=<span class="hljs-string">'binary_crossentropy'</span>)
<span class="hljs-comment"># Assume the model is trained here</span>

<span class="hljs-comment"># Save the model locally</span>
model.save(<span class="hljs-string">"model_v1.h5"</span>)  <span class="hljs-comment"># Save in HDF5 format</span>
</code></div></div></pre><p>The file <code>model_v1.h5</code> is saved in your current working directory.</p><h4><strong>Example with Scikit-learn</strong></h4><pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">python</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-python"><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> sklearn.ensemble <span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> RandomForestClassifier

<span class="hljs-comment"># Preprocess the image</span>

</code></div></div></pre><h4><strong>4. Make Predictions</strong></h4><pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">python</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-python"><span class="hljs-comment"># Predict the class of the input image</span>

<span class="hljs-comment"># Get the class label</span>
class_index = np.argmax(predictions, axis=<span class="hljs-number">1</span>)  <span class="hljs-comment"># Index of the highest probability</span>
<span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">f"Predicted class index: <span class="hljs-subst">{class_index}</span>"</span>)

<span class="hljs-comment"># If you have a label mapping</span>
class_labels = [<span class="hljs-string">"Class A"</span>, <span class="hljs-string">"Class B"</span>, <span class="hljs-string">"Class C"</span>]  <span class="hljs-comment"># Replace with your labels</span>
predicted_label = class_labels[class_index[<span class="hljs-number">0</span>]]
<span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">f"Predicted class label: <span class="hljs-subst">{predicted_label}</span>"</span>)
</code></div></div></pre><hr><h3><strong>Key Points</strong></h3><ol><li><p><strong>Model Input Shape</strong></p><ul><li>Ensure the input image size matches the models input shape (e.g., 224x224 if using a pretrained model like ResNet).</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Label Mapping</strong></p><ul><li>If your dataset had class labels (e.g., <code>0 = Cat</code>, <code>1 = Dog</code>), maintain a mapping to interpret the predicted class index.</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Normalization</strong></p><ul><li>Normalize the input image in the same way as the training data (e.g., divide pixel values by 255 if you did this during training).</li></ul></li></ol><hr><h3><strong>Example Output</strong></h3><p>For an input image:</p><ul><li>The model predicts probabilities for each class, e.g., <code>[0.1, 0.3, 0.6]</code>.</li><li><code>np.argmax</code> selects the class with the highest probability (e.g., index <code>2</code> with <code>0.6</code>).</li><li>The label mapping (<code>["Class A", "Class B", "Class C"]</code>) maps index <code>2</code> to <code>Class C</code>.</li></ul><hr><p>Let me know if you need more details or have issues with a specific language-python"><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> tensorflow.keras.models <span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> load_model
<span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> tensorflow.keras.preprocessing.image <span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> load_img, img_to_array

<span class="hljs-comment"># Load the trained model</span>

from tensorflow.keras.preprocessing.image import load_img, img_to_array
import numpy as np

# Load the trained model
model = load_model("//content//cnn.h5")  # Replace with your model file

# Preprocess the input image
image_path = "drive//MyDrive//heartimages//Normal Person ECG Images (284x12=3408)//Normal(1).jpg"  # Replace with the path to the new image
img = load_img(image_path, target_size=(256, 256))  # Resize to match the model input shape (256, 256)
img_array = img_to_array(img)
img_array = np.expand_dims(img_array, axis=0)  # Add batch dimension
img_array = img_array / 255.0  # Normalize pixel values

# Make predictions
prediction = model.predict(img_array)
predicted_class = np.argmax(prediction, axis=1)

# Map the prediction to a class label
class_labels = ['Myocardial Infarction', 'History of MI', 'Abnormal Heartbeat', 'Normal'] # Adjust as per your dataset
diagnosis = class_labels[predicted_class[0]]
print("Diagnosis:", diagnosis)

class="markdown prose w-full break-words dark:prose-invert dark"><p>To map the predictions to a class label in your case, you need to ensure that the <strong>output layer of your model</strong> corresponds to the number of classes in your dataset and that the order of the <code>class_labels</code> list matches the order in which your model was trained. Here's how it works:</p><hr><h3><strong>How <code>np.argmax</code> Maps Predictions</strong></h3><ol><li><p><strong>Predictions Output</strong><br>The <code>model.predict(img_array)</code> function outputs an array of probabilities for each class. For example:</p><pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">python</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-python">prediction = [[<span class="hljs-number">0.1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0.2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0.6</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0.1</span>]]
</code></div></div></pre><ul><li>This array indicates the models confidence in each class. In this case, the highest probability is <code>0.6</code> for the third class (<code>index = 2</code>).</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Class Index to Label Mapping</strong><br>Use <code>np.argmax(prediction, axis=1)</code> to get the index of the class with the highest probability:</p><pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">python</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-python">predicted_class = np.argmax(prediction, axis=<span class="hljs-number">1</span>)  <span class="hljs-comment"># Output: [2]</span>
</code></div></div></pre><ul><li>This corresponds to the third class in your <code>class_labels</code> list.</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Mapping to Class Labels</strong><br>Use the index to retrieve the class label:</p><pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">python</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-python">diagnosis = class_labels[predicted_class[<span class="hljs-number">0</span>]]  <span class="hljs-comment"># Output: "Abnormal Heartbeat"</span>
</code></div></div></pre></li></ol><hr><h3><strong>Ensure Correct Class Labels</strong></h3><p>Your <code>class_labels</code> list must match the order of the output neurons in your model's final layer. For example:</p><ul><li>If your model was trained with labels <code>[0, 1, 2, 3]</code> representing <code>['Myocardial Infarction', 'History of MI', 'Abnormal Heartbeat', 'Normal']</code>, ensure that:<pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">python</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-python">class_labels = [<span class="hljs-string">'Myocardial Infarction'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'History of MI'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'Abnormal Heartbeat'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'Normal'</span>]
</code></div></div></pre></li></ul><hr><h3><strong>Validation of Predicted Class</strong></h3><p>To debug or confirm correctness:</p><ol><li><p><strong>Print Probabilities</strong>:</p><pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">python</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-python"><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Prediction probabilities:"</span>, prediction)
</code></div></div></pre><p>This shows how confident the model is for each class.</p></li><li><p><strong>Verify Class Index</strong>:</p><pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">python</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-python"><span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Predicted class index:"</span>, predicted_class[<span class="hljs-number">0</span>])
<span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Corresponding class label:"</span>, class_labels[predicted_class[<span class="hljs-number">0</span>]])
</code></div></div></pre></li></ol><hr><h3><strong>Complete Code Example</strong></h3><pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">python</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-python"><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> tensorflow.keras.models <span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> load_model
<span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> tensorflow.keras.preprocessing.image <span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> load_img, img_to_array
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> numpy <span class="hljs-keyword">as</span> np

<span class="hljs-comment"># Load the trained model</span>
model = load_model(<span class="hljs-string">"//content//cnn.h5"</span>)  <span class="hljs-comment"># Replace with your model file</span>

<span class="hljs-comment"># Preprocess the input image</span>
image_path = <span class="hljs-string">"drive//MyDrive//heartimages//Normal Person ECG Images (284x12=3408)//Normal(1).jpg"</span>  <span class="hljs-comment"># Replace with the path to the new image</span>
img = load_img(image_path, target_size=(<span class="hljs-number">256</span>, <span class="hljs-number">256</span>))  <span class="hljs-comment"># Resize to match the model input shape</span>
img_array = img_to_array(img)
img_array = np.expand_dims(img_array, axis=<span class="hljs-number">0</span>)  <span class="hljs-comment"># Add batch dimension</span>
img_array = img_array / <span class="hljs-number">255.0</span>  <span class="hljs-comment"># Normalize pixel values</span>

<span class="hljs-comment"># Make predictions</span>
prediction = model.predict(img_array)
predicted_class = np.argmax(prediction, axis=<span class="hljs-number">1</span>)  <span class="hljs-comment"># Get class index</span>

<span class="hljs-comment"># Map the prediction to a class label</span>
class_labels = [<span class="hljs-string">'Myocardial Infarction'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'History of MI'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'Abnormal Heartbeat'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'Normal'</span>]
diagnosis = class_labels[predicted_class[<span class="hljs-number">0</span>]]

<span class="hljs-comment"># Print results</span>
<span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Prediction probabilities:"</span>, prediction)
<span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Predicted class index:"</span>, predicted_class[<span class="hljs-number">0</span>])
<span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Diagnosis:"</span>, diagnosis)
</code></div></div></pre><hr><h3><strong>Output Example</strong></h3><p>For an input image, the output might be:</p><pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">lua</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-lua">Prediction probabilities: <span class="hljs-string">[[0.1, 0.2, 0.6, 0.1]]</span>
Predicted class index: <span class="hljs-number">2</span>
Diagnosis: Abnormal Heartbeat
</code></div></div></pre><hr><p>This approach ensures that your predictions are accurately mapped to human-readable labels. data-message-author-role="assistant" data-message-id="68d12add-dbda-4175-8db7-588e972926cd" dir="auto" class="min-h-8 text-message flex w-full flex-col items-end gap-2 whitespace-normal break-words dark:prose-invert dark"><p>If your class labels and the model's class labels are the same, it means the models output corresponds to the class labels in the same order as they were used during training. In this case, you don't need to worry about reordering the labels when predicting. Heres how you can confirm and proceed:</p><h3><strong>Steps to Ensure Correct Mapping:</strong></h3><ol><li><p><strong>Check the Training Process:</strong></p><ul><li>During training, the classes were assigned in a specific order (e.g., 'Myocardial Infarction', 'History of MI', 'Abnormal Heartbeat', 'Normal').</li><li>The model will output the predicted class index in the same order as the classes were assigned during training.</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Match the Class Labels:</strong></p><ul><li>When you save the trained model and load it, the class labels should remain consistent, meaning the prediction output index will directly map to the class label.</li></ul></li></ol><h3><strong>Complete Prediction Code with Class Label Mapping:</strong></h3><pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">python</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-python"><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> tensorflow.keras.models <span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> load_model
<span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> tensorflow.keras.preprocessing.image <span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> load_img, img_to_array
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> numpy <span class="hljs-keyword">as</span> np

<span class="hljs-comment"># Load the trained model</span>
model = load_model(<span class="hljs-string">"path_to_your_model.h5"</span>)  <span class="hljs-comment"># Replace with the correct model path</span>

<span class="hljs-comment"># Preprocess the input image</span>
image_path = <span class="hljs-string">"path_to_your_image.jpg"</span>  <span class="hljs-comment"># Replace with the correct image path</span>
img = load_img(image_path, target_size=(<span class="hljs-number">256</span>, <span class="hljs-number">256</span>))  <span class="hljs-comment"># Resize to match the model input shape</span>
img_array = img_to_array(img)
img_array = np.expand_dims(img_array, axis=<span class="hljs-number">0</span>)  <span class="hljs-comment"># Add batch dimension</span>
img_array = img_array / <span class="hljs-number">255.0</span>  <span class="hljs-comment"># Normalize pixel values</span>

<span class="hljs-comment"># Make predictions</span>
prediction = model.predict(img_array)
predicted_class = np.argmax(prediction, axis=<span class="hljs-number">1</span>)  <span class="hljs-comment"># Get class index</span>

<span class="hljs-comment"># Class labels used during training (must match the order used during training)</span>
class_labels = [<span class="hljs-string">'Myocardial Infarction'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'History of MI'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'Abnormal Heartbeat'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'Normal'</span>]

<span class="hljs-comment"># Map the predicted index to the corresponding class label</span>
diagnosis = class_labels[predicted_class[<span class="hljs-number">0</span>]]

<span class="hljs-comment"># Print the results</span>
<span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Prediction probabilities:"</span>, prediction)
<span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Predicted class index:"</span>, predicted_class[<span class="hljs-number">0</span>])
<span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Diagnosis:"</span>, diagnosis)
</code></div></div></pre><h3><strong>Explanation of the Code:</strong></h3><ol><li><p><strong>Model Prediction:</strong></p><ul><li>The model outputs an array of probabilities, one for each class.</li><li>We use <code>np.argmax(prediction, axis=1)</code> to find the index of the class with the highest probability.</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Mapping Index to Class Label:</strong></p><ul><li>The <code>predicted_class[0]</code> gives the index of the predicted class.</li><li>We use this index to map it to the corresponding class in <code>class_labels</code>.</li></ul></li></ol><h3><strong>Example Output:</strong></h3><p>For an image input, the output might be:</p><pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div Predicted class index: <span class="hljs-number">2</span>
Diagnosis: Abnormal Heartbeat
</code></div></div></pre><p>This confirms that your model is correctly mapping the predicted index to the class labels.</p><h3><strong>Troubleshooting Tips:</strong></h3><ul><li><strong>If the predictions are incorrect</strong> (e.g., misclassification), double-check:<ul><li>The model was trained properly with correct labels.</li><li>The input image is preprocessed in the same way as the training images (e.g., same resizing, normalization).</li></ul></li><li><strong>Ensure the class labels are the same order</strong> as during the training phase.</li></ul><hr><p>Let me know if you from tensorflow.keras.preprocessing.image import load_img, img_to_array
import numpy as np

# Load the trained model
model = load_model("/content/sample_data/cnn1_model.h5")   # Replace with the correct model path

# Preprocess the input image
image_path = "drive/MyDrive/heartimages/ECG Images of Myocardial Infarction Patients (240x12=2880)/MI(101).jpg" # Replace with the correct image path
img = load_img(image_path, target_size=(256, 256))  # Resize to match the model input shape
img_array = img_to_array(img)
img_array = np.expand_dims(img_array, axis=0)  # Add batch dimension
img_array = img_array / 255.0  # Normalize pixel values

# Make predictions
prediction = model.predict(img_array)
predicted_class = np.argmax(prediction, axis=1)  # Get class index

# Class labels used during training (must match the order used during training)
class_labels = ['Myocardial Infarction', 'History of MI', 'Abnormal Heartbeat', 'Normal']

# Map the predicted index to the corresponding class label
diagnosis = class_labels[predicted_class[0]]

# Print the results
print("Prediction probabilities:", prediction)
print("Predicted class index:", predicted_class[0])
print("Diagnosis:", diagnosis)

class="markdown prose w-full break-words dark:prose-invert dark"><p>To <strong>add images to a trained Convolutional Neural Network (CNN)</strong> for prediction, follow these steps to ensure the This includes preprocessing, handling input dimensions, and ensuring compatibility with the trained model.</p><hr><h3><strong>Steps to Prepare and Use Images for Prediction:</strong></h3><ol><li><p><strong>Prepare Your Dataset:</strong>
Ensure the images you want to predict are properly formatted. The steps include:</p><ul><li>Images should be resized to the same dimensions used during training (e.g., <code>256x256</code> in your code).</li><li>Images should be normalized if normalization was used during training (e.g., dividing pixel values by <code>255.0</code>).</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Ensure Labels Match:</strong>

    <span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"-"</span> * <span class="hljs-number">50</span>)
</code></div></div></pre></li></ol><hr><h3><strong>Enhancements for Better Predictions:</strong></h3><ol><li><p><strong>Batch Processing</strong>:
If you have a large number of images, you can process them in a batch to save time:</p><pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">python</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-python"><span class="hljs-keyword">def</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">preprocess_image</span>(<span class="hljs-params">image_path</span>):
    img = load_img(image_path, target_size=(<span class="hljs-number">256</span>, <span class="hljs-number">256</span>))
    img_array = img_to_array(img)
    img_array = img_array / <span class="hljs-number">255.0</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> img_array

<span class="hljs-comment"># Preprocess all images</span>
image_arrays = np.array([preprocess_image(img_path) <span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> img_path <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> image_paths])

<span class="hljs-comment"># Predict in batch</span>
predictions = model.predict(image_arrays)

<span class="hljs-comment"># Map predictions to class labels</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> idx, prediction <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">enumerate</span>(predictions):
    predicted_class = np.argmax(prediction)
    diagnosis = class_labels[predicted_class]
    <span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">f"Image: <span class="hljs-subst">{image_paths[idx]}</span>"</span>)
    <span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Diagnosis:"</span>, diagnosis)
</code></div></div></pre></li><li><p><strong>Handle Misclassified Images</strong>:
If predictions seem inaccurate:</p><ul><li>Verify the preprocessing steps (e.g., image size and normalization).</li><li>Check if the dataset used for training is balanced across classes.</li><li>Consider retraining or fine-tuning the model with more representative data.</li></ul></li></ol><hr><h3><strong>Next Steps</strong>:</h3><ul><li>Ensure the input image paths are data-message-author-role="assistant" data-message-id="e61edcb3-75ef-41c6-9efe-09d3312bf9b7" dir="auto" class="min-h-8 text-message flex w-full flex-col items-end gap-2 whitespace-normal break-words dark:prose-invert dark"><p>Here is the full code for predicting the class of multiple input images using a trained CNN model:</p><pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-python"><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> tensorflow.keras.models <span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> load_model
<span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> tensorflow.keras.preprocessing.image <span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> load_img, img_to_array
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> numpy <span class="hljs-keyword">as</span> np

<span class="hljs-comment"># Load the trained model</span>
model = load_model(<span class="hljs-string">"/content/sample_data/cnn1_model.h5"</span>)  <span class="hljs-comment"># Replace with your model's path</span>

<span class="hljs-comment"># Class labels (must match the order used during training)</span>
class_labels = [<span class="hljs-string">'Myocardial Infarction'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'History of MI'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'Abnormal Heartbeat'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'Normal'</span>]

<span class="hljs-comment"># List of image paths to predict</span>
image_paths = [
    <span class="hljs-string">"drive/MyDrive/heartimages/ECG Images of Myocardial Infarction Patients (240x12=2880)/MI(101).jpg"</span>,
    <span class="hljs-string">"drive/MyDrive/heartimages/Normal Person ECG Images (284x12=3408)/Normal(1).jpg"</span>
]

<span class="hljs-comment"># Function to preprocess a single image</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">def</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">preprocess_image</span>(<span class="hljs-params">image_path</span>):
    img = load_img(image_path, target_size=(<span class="hljs-number">256</span>, <span class="hljs-number">256</span>))  <span class="hljs-comment"># Resize to match model input</span>
    img_array = img_to_array(img)
    img_array = img_array / <span class="hljs-number">255.0</span>  <span class="hljs-comment"># Normalize pixel values</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> np.expand_dims(img_array, axis=<span class="hljs-number">0</span>)  <span class="hljs-comment"># Add batch dimension</span>

<span class="hljs-comment"># Predict and display results for each image</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> image_path <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> image_paths:
    img_array = preprocess_image(image_path)
    prediction = model.predict(img_array)  <span class="hljs-comment"># Predict probabilities</span>
    predicted_class = np.argmax(prediction, axis=<span class="hljs-number">1</span>)[<span class="hljs-number">0</span>]  <span class="hljs-comment"># Get class index</span>
    diagnosis = class_labels[predicted_class]  <span class="hljs-comment"># Map index to class label</span>
    <span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">f"Image: <span class="hljs-subst">{image_path}</span>"</span>)
    <span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Prediction probabilities:"</span>, prediction)
    <span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">f"Predicted class index: <span class="hljs-subst">{predicted_class}</span>"</span>)
    <span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">f"Diagnosis: <span class="hljs-subst">{diagnosis}</span>"</span>)
    <span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"-"</span> * <span class="hljs-number">50</span>)
</code></div></div></pre><h3>Key Notes:</h3><ol><li>Replace the model path (<code>/content/sample_data/cnn1_model.h5</code>) with the actual location of your saved model.</li><li>Update the <code>image_paths</code> list with the paths to your input images.</li><li>The <code>class_labels</code> list should match the exact order used during training.</li></ol><p>This code will process each image, make predictions, and print the results (class probabilities, predicted index, and diagnosis).</p></div></div></div></div><div class="mb-2 flex gap-3 empty:hidden -ml-2"><div class="flex max-w-full flex-col flex-grow"><div data-message-author-role="assistant" data-message-id="f9e9d48c-2c7d-4fb5-8d61-c437766e7396" dir="auto" class="min-h-8 text-message flex w-full flex-col class="markdown prose w-full break-words dark:prose-invert dark"><p>If your model is not giving satisfactory predictions, here are a few possible reasons and their solutions:</p><hr><h3><strong>1. Issues with Model Training</strong></h3><ul><li><strong>Problem</strong>: The model might not have learned the features of the classes effectively due to insufficient training data, an imbalanced dataset, or overfitting.</li><li><strong>Solution</strong>:<ul><li>Ensure you have sufficient and diverse data for each class.</li><li>Use data augmentation techniques to increase dataset variability.</li><li>Regularize the model using dropout or L2 regularization during training.</li><li>Check the training and validation accuracy to see if overfitting occurred.</li></ul></li></ul><hr><h3><strong>2. Incorrect Preprocessing</strong></h3><ul><li><strong>Problem</strong>: The input images may not be preprocessed in the same way as during training.</li><li><strong>Solution</strong>:<ul><li>Ensure the images are resized to the correct dimensions (e.g., <code>256x256</code>).</li><li>Verify if normalization (e.g., dividing pixel values by 255) matches the preprocessing used during training.</li><li>Double-check for any data augmentations (rotation, flipping) applied during training.</li></ul></li></ul><hr><h3><strong>3. Confusion Between Classes</strong></h3><ul><li><strong>Problem</strong>: Similar features between classes like 'Abnormal Heartbeat' and 'Normal' may cause confusion.</li><li><strong>Solution</strong>:<ul><li>Analyze the confusion matrix to identify where the model struggles.</li><li>Consider combining similar classes or adding features that help distinguish them better.</li></ul></li></ul><hr><h3><strong>4. Model Architecture and Hyperparameters</strong></h3><ul><li><strong>Problem</strong>: The CNN architecture might not be complex enough to capture the features of the dataset.</li><li><strong>Solution</strong>:<ul><li>Use a pre-trained model (like VGG16, ResNet) with transfer learning for better performance.</li><li>Experiment with different CNN architectures and hyperparameters (e.g., learning rate, number of layers).</li></ul></li></ul><hr><h3><strong>5. Handling Predictions</strong></h3><ul><li><strong>Problem</strong>: The predicted probabilities are close together, indicating the model is uncertain.</li><li><strong>Solution</strong>:<ul><li>Use a confidence threshold. If the maximum probability is below a certain value (e.g., 0.6), classify it as "uncertain."</li><li>Example:<pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">python</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-python">max_prob = np.<span class="hljs-built_in">max</span>(prediction)
<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> max_prob &lt; <span class="hljs-number">0.6</span>:
    diagnosis = <span class="hljs-string">"Uncertain"</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">else</span>:
    predicted_class = np.argmax(prediction, axis=<span class="hljs-number">1</span>)[<span class="hljs-number">0</span>]
    diagnosis = class_labels[predicted_class]
</code></div></div></pre></li></ul></li></ul><hr><h3><strong>6. Evaluate and Improve the Model</strong></h3><ul><li><strong>Steps to Evaluate</strong>:<ul><li>Check the confusion matrix on the test set to evaluate class-wise performance.</li><li>Compute metrics like precision, recall, F1-score, and ROC-AUC.</li></ul></li><li><strong>Steps to Improve</strong>:<ul><li>Retrain the model on a balanced or augmented dataset.</li><li>Fine-tune the model by freezing lower layers and training only the top layers (for transfer learning).</li></ul></li></ul><hr><h3><strong>Next Steps for Diagnosis</strong></h3><ol><li>Evaluate your model using a test set or validation set to identify performance issues.</li><li>Ensure input preprocessing (image resizing, normalization) is consistent between training and inference.</li><li>If issues persist, consider class="group/conversation-turn relative flex w-full min-w-0 flex-col agent-turn"><div class="flex-col gap-1 md:gap-3"><div class="flex max-w-full flex-col flex-grow"><div data-message-author-role="assistant" data-message-id="9292b1f5-851e-49b9-beeb-8a14b2409ec1" dir="auto" class="min-h-8 text-message flex w-full flex-col items-end gap-2 whitespace-normal break-words text-start [.text-message+&amp;]:mt-5" data-message-model-slug="gpt-4o"><div class="flex w-full flex-col gap-1 empty:hidden first:pt-[3px]"><div class="markdown prose w-full break-words dark:prose-invert dark"><p>Getting 100% training accuracy but poor predictions on unseen images indicates <strong>overfitting</strong>your model has memorized the training data but failed to generalize to new data. Here's how to address this issue:</p><hr><h3><strong>1. Evaluate Performance on a Validation/Test Set</strong></h3><ul><li><strong>Check if validation accuracy is high</strong>: If validation accuracy is much lower than training accuracy, overfitting is confirmed.</li><li><strong>Steps</strong>:<ul><li>Split your dataset into training, validation, and test sets.</li><li>Evaluate the model on the validation set to ensure it generalizes well.</li></ul></li></ul><hr><h3><strong>2. Use Data Augmentation</strong></h3><ul><li>Add variability to your training data to help the model generalize better.</li><li>Example:<pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">python</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-python"><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> tensorflow.keras.preprocessing.image <span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> ImageDataGenerator

datagen = ImageDataGenerator(
    rotation_range=<span class="hljs-number">20</span>,
    width_shift_range=<span class="hljs-number">0.2</span>,
    height_shift_range=<span class="hljs-number">0.2</span>,
    shear_range=<span class="hljs-number">0.2</span>,
    zoom_range=<span class="hljs-number">0.2</span>,
    horizontal_flip=<span class="hljs-literal">True</span>,
    fill_mode=<span class="hljs-string">'nearest'</span>
)
datagen.fit(train_images)  <span class="hljs-comment"># Apply on training data</span>
</code></div></div></pre></li></ul><hr><h3><strong>3. Use Regularization Techniques</strong></h3><ul><li>Add <strong>dropout layers</strong> in your model:<pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">python</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-python"><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> tensorflow.keras.layers <span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> Dropout

model.add(Dropout(<span class="hljs-number">0.5</span>))  <span class="hljs-comment"># Drop 50% of neurons during training</span>
</code></div></div></pre></li><li>Apply <strong>L2 Regularization</strong>:<pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">python</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-python"><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> tensorflow.keras.regularizers <span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> l2

model.add(Dense(units, activation=<span class="hljs-string">'relu'</span>, kernel_regularizer=l2(<span class="hljs-number">0.01</span>)))
</code></div></div></pre></li></ul><hr><h3><strong>4. Fine-Tune Learning Rate and Epochs</strong></h3><ul><li>Reduce the learning rate to prevent large updates to weights.</li><li>Stop training before overfitting occurs using <strong>early stopping</strong>:<pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">python</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-python"><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> tensorflow.keras.callbacks <span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> EarlyStopping

early_stopping = EarlyStopping(monitor=<span class="hljs-string">'val_loss'</span>, patience=<span class="hljs-number">5</span>, restore_best_weights=<span class="hljs-literal">True</span>)
model.fit(train_images, train_labels, validation_data=(val_images, val_labels), callbacks=[early_stopping])
</code></div></div></pre></li></ul><hr><h3><strong>5. Use Transfer Learning</strong></h3><ul><li>Leverage a pre-trained model (e.g., VGG16, ResNet) instead of training from scratch. Fine-tune the last few layers with your dataset:<pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">python</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-python"><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> tensorflow.keras.applications <span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> VGG16

base_model = VGG16(weights=<span class="hljs-string">'imagenet'</span>, include_top=<span class="hljs-literal">False</span>, input_shape=(<span class="hljs-number">256</span>, <span class="hljs-number">256</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>))
<span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> layer <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> base_model.layers:
    layer.trainable = <span class="hljs-literal">False</span>  <span class="hljs-comment"># Freeze pre-trained layers</span>

model = Sequential([
    base_model,
    Flatten(),
    Dense(<span class="hljs-number">128</span>, activation=<span class="hljs-string">'relu'</span>),
    Dropout(<span class="hljs-number">0.5</span>),
    Dense(<span class="hljs-built_in">len</span>(class_labels), activation=<span class="hljs-string">'softmax'</span>)
])
</code></div></div></pre></li></ul><hr><h3><strong>6. Improve Testing Pipeline</strong></h3><p>Ensure that the input image for testing is preprocessed identically to the training images:</p><ul><li>Resizing</li><li>Normalizing (divide by 255.0)</li><li>Applying augmentations used during training</li></ul><hr><h3><strong>7. Evaluate Class-Wise Predictions</strong></h3><ul><li>Use a <strong>confusion matrix</strong> to see which classes the model confuses most.<pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">python</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-python"><span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> sklearn.metrics <span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> confusion_matrix, classification_report

y_pred = np.argmax(model.predict(test_images), axis=<span class="hljs-number">1</span>)
<span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(confusion_matrix(test_labels, y_pred))
<span class="hljs-built_in">print</span>(classification_report(test_labels, y_pred))
</code></div></div></pre></li></ul><hr><h3><strong>8. Diagnose with Misclassified Images</strong></h3><p>Analyze a few misclassified images to identify patterns:</p><ul><li>Does the image quality differ from training images?</li><li>Are there ambiguous cases in the dataset?</li></ul><hr><h3><strong>9. Gradually Increase Complexity</strong></h3><p>If youre building your own CNN, start with a simple architecture and slowly add layers to avoid overfitting:</p><pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">python</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-python">model = Sequential([
    Conv2D(<span class="hljs-number">32</span>, (<span class="hljs-number">3</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>), activation=<span class="hljs-string">'relu'</span>, input_shape=(<span class="hljs-number">256</span>, <span class="hljs-number">256</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>)),
    MaxPooling2D((<span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>)),
    Dropout(<span class="hljs-number">0.25</span>),
    Flatten(),
    Dense(<span class="hljs-number">128</span>, activation=<span class="hljs-string">'relu'</span>),
    Dropout(<span class="hljs-number">0.5</span>),
    Dense(<span class="hljs-built_in">len</span>(class_labels), activation=<span class="hljs-string">'softmax'</span>)
])
</code></div></div></pre><hr><h3><strong>10. Re-train the Model</strong></h3><ul><li>Incorporate all the above techniques and retrain the model.</li><li>Monitor the training and validation loss to ensure proper convergence.</li></ul><hr><h3><strong>Expected Outcomes</strong></h3><ul><li>Lower training accuracy (typically &lt; 100%) but significantly improved validation accuracy.</li><li>Better generalization to unseen images with meaningful predictions.</li></ul><p>Let me know if you want detailed examples for any specific step!</p></div></div></div></div><div class="mb-2 flex gap-3 empty:hidden from tensorflow.keras.preprocessing.image import load_img, img_to_array
import numpy as np

# Load the trained model
model = load_model("/content/sample_data/cnn1_model.h5")  # Replace with your model's path

# Class labels (must match the order used during training)
class_labels = ['Myocardial Infarction', 'History of MI', 'Abnormal Heartbeat', 'Normal']

# List of image paths to predict
image_paths = [
    "drive/MyDrive/heartimages/ECG Images of Myocardial Infarction Patients (240x12=2880)/MI(101).jpg",
    "drive/MyDrive/heartimages/Normal Person ECG Images (284x12=3408)/Normal(1).jpg"
]

# Function to preprocess a single image
def preprocess_image(image_path):
    img = load_img(image_path, target_size=(256, 256))  # Resize to match model input
    img_array = img_to_array(img)
    img_array = img_array / 255.0  # Normalize pixel values
    return np.expand_dims(img_array, axis=0)  # Add batch dimension

# Predict and display results for each image
for image_path in image_paths:
    img_array = preprocess_image(image_path)
    prediction = model.predict(img_array)  # Predict probabilities
    predicted_class = np.argmax(prediction, axis=1)[0]  # Get class index
    diagnosis = class_labels[predicted_class]  # Map index to class label
    print(f"Image: {image_path}")
    print("Prediction probabilities:", prediction)
    print(f"Predicted class index: {predicted_class}")
    print(f"Diagnosis: {diagnosis}")
    print("-" * 50)
