class="group/conversation-turn relative flex w-full min-w-0 flex-col agent-turn"><div class="flex-col gap-1 md:gap-3"><div class="flex max-w-full flex-col flex-grow"><div data-message-author-role="assistant" data-message-id="ecac1e46-d473-41cb-a7ff-20e8c208ae60" dir="auto" class="min-h-8 text-message flex w-full flex-col items-end gap-2 whitespace-normal break-words text-start [.text-message+&amp;]:mt-5" data-message-model-slug="gpt-4o"><div class="flex w-full flex-col gap-1 empty:hidden first:pt-[3px]"><div class="markdown prose w-full break-words dark:prose-invert dark"><p>To integrate the prediction functionality into a <strong>Streamlit</strong> interface, we can create a web application where users can upload an image, and the app will classify it using the trained CNN model. Below is the modified code for a Streamlit-based interface:</p><hr><h3><strong>Streamlit Code</strong></h3><pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">python</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-python"><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> streamlit <span class="hljs-keyword">as</span> st
<span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> tensorflow.keras.models <span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> load_model
<span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> tensorflow.keras.preprocessing.image <span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> load_img, img_to_array
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> numpy <span class="hljs-keyword">as</span> np

<span class="hljs-comment"># Load the trained model</span>
model = load_model(<span class="hljs-string">"/content/sample_data/cnn1_model.h5"</span>)  <span class="hljs-comment"># Replace with your model path</span>

<span class="hljs-comment"># Class labels (must match the order used during training)</span>
class_labels = [<span class="hljs-string">'Myocardial Infarction'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'History of MI'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'Abnormal Heartbeat'</span>, <span class="hljs-string">'Normal'</span>]

<span class="hljs-comment"># Function to preprocess the image</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">def</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">preprocess_image</span>(<span class="hljs-params">image</span>):
    img = load_img(image, target_size=(<span class="hljs-number">256</span>, <span class="hljs-number">256</span>))  <span class="hljs-comment"># Resize to match model input</span>
    img_array = img_to_array(img)
    img_array = img_array / <span class="hljs-number">255.0</span>  <span class="hljs-comment"># Normalize pixel values</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> np.expand_dims(img_array, axis=<span class="hljs-number">0</span>)  <span class="hljs-comment"># Add batch dimension</span>

<span class="hljs-comment"># Streamlit UI</span>
st.title(<span class="hljs-string">"Cardiovascular Disease Classification"</span>)
st.write(<span class="hljs-string">"Upload an ECG image to classify the condition."</span>)

<span class="hljs-comment"># File uploader widget</span>
uploaded_file = st.file_uploader(<span class="hljs-string">"Choose an image file"</span>, <span class="hljs-built_in">type</span>=[<span class="hljs-string">"jpg"</span>, <span class="hljs-string">"jpeg"</span>, <span class="hljs-string">"png"</span>])

<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> uploaded_file <span class="hljs-keyword">is</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">not</span> <span class="hljs-literal">None</span>:
    <span class="hljs-comment"># Display the uploaded image</span>
    st.image(uploaded_file, caption=<span class="hljs-string">"Uploaded ECG Image"</span>, use_column_width=<span class="hljs-literal">True</span>)
    st.write(<span class="hljs-string">"Classifying..."</span>)

    <span class="hljs-comment"># Preprocess and predict</span>
    img_array = preprocess_image(uploaded_file)
    prediction = model.predict(img_array)
    predicted_class = np.argmax(prediction, axis=<span class="hljs-number">1</span>)[<span class="hljs-number">0</span>]
    diagnosis = class_labels[predicted_class]

    <span class="hljs-comment"># Display results</span>
    st.write(<span class="hljs-string">"### Diagnosis:"</span>)
    st.write(<span class="hljs-string">f"**<span class="hljs-subst">{diagnosis}</span>**"</span>)
    st.write(<span class="hljs-string">"### Prediction Probabilities:"</span>)
    <span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> i, label <span class="hljs-keyword">in</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">enumerate</span>(class_labels):
        st.write(<span class="hljs-string">f"<span class="hljs-subst">{label}</span>: <span class="hljs-subst">{prediction[<span class="hljs-number">0</span>][i]:<span class="hljs-number">.2</span>f}</span>"</span>)
</code></div></div></pre><hr><h3><strong>Steps to Run the App</strong></h3><ol><li><p><strong>Install Dependencies</strong>:
Ensure that Streamlit is installed:</p><pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">bash</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-bash">pip install streamlit tensorflow

(GCP)</strong>, or <strong>AWS</strong>. The simplest and most popular method for Streamlit apps is using <strong>Streamlit Community Cloud</strong>. Below are the steps for deployment:</p><hr><h3><strong>1. Deploying with Streamlit Community Cloud</strong></h3><p>Streamlit Community Cloud is free and designed for Streamlit apps.</p><h4><strong>Steps</strong>:</h4><ol><li><p><strong>Prepare Your Project</strong>:</p><ul><li>Ensure your <code>app.py</code> file (your Streamlit script) is in a folder with all required dependencies listed in a <code>requirements.txt</code> file.</li><li>Create a <code>requirements.txt</code> file:<pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">plaintext</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-plaintext">streamlit

</code></div></div></pre>Add any additional libraries you use.</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Push Your Code to GitHub</strong>:</p><ul><li>Create a GitHub repository and upload your project files (e.g., <code>app.py</code>, <code>requirements.txt</code>, and the model file <code>cnn1_model.h5</code>).</li><li>Make sure your model file is included in the repository.</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Sign In to Streamlit Community Cloud</strong>:</p><ul><li>Go to <a rel="noopener" target="_new" style="--streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-1); --animation-rate: var(--batch-play-rate-1);"><span style="--animation-count: 1; --streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-2);">Streamlit</span><span style="--animation-count: 2; --streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-2);"> Community</span><span style="--animation-count: 3; --streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-2);"> Cloud</span></a> and log in with your GitHub account.</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Deploy Your App</strong>:</p><ul><li>Click on <strong>"New App"</strong> and link your GitHub repository.</li><li>Select the branch and the main script file (<code>app.py</code>).</li><li>Click <strong>Deploy</strong>.</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Access Your App</strong>:</p><ul><li>Once deployed, Streamlit will provide you with a public URL to share your app.</li></ul></li></ol><hr><h3><strong>2. Follow these steps:</p><ol><li><p><strong>Create a GitHub Account</strong>:</p><ul><li>Go to <a rel="noopener" target="_new" href="https://github.com/" style="--streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-1); --animation-rate: var(--batch-play-rate-1);"><span style="--animation-count: 5; --streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-2);">GitHub</span></a> and sign up for a free account.</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Create a New Repository</strong>:</p><ul><li>After logging in, click on the <strong>+</strong> button in the top-right corner and select <strong>New Repository</strong>.</li><li>Name your repository (e.g., <code>cardiovascular-disease-app</code>) and click <strong>Create repository</strong>.</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Upload Your Files</strong>:</p><ul><li>On the repository page, click <strong>Add file &gt; Upload files</strong>.</li><li>Drag and drop all your project files (including <code>app.py</code>, <code>requirements.txt</code>, and the model file).</li><li>Click <strong>Commit changes</strong> to save the files to GitHub.</li></ul></li></ol><hr><h4><strong>3.
